 andhra pradesh kii duusari loksabhaa siton kii tarah ongol loksabhaa seat bhi kabhi congress kaa kaa garh tha
 The Congress has won this seat 11 times since 1952
 2014 main is seat se YSR congress ke vivi subba reddy chunaav jite the, unhone tidipi ke shrinivasulu reddy ko chunaav main haraaya tha
 This time Subba Reddy is not contesting the election
 wiesar congress ne is baar shrinivasulu reddy ko tikat diya he
 While TDP has given ticket from this seat to Siddha Radhav Rao
 sidda raghav raav chandrababu naidu cabinet main mantri the

 bhartiya janata party is seat se thongti shrinivasulu ko tikat diya he
 Janasena Party has nominated Saibabu as its candidate from this seat
 is seat se badi sankhya main nirdaleey bhi chunaav lard rahe hai
 Political background: This seat was initially won by independents 2 times
 iske baad 1957 main congress ne is seat ko apane kheme main kar liya
 In the general election held in 1962, the Communist Party of India won it
 do baar tidipi, do baar nirdaleey or ek baar communist party of india ke ummidavaaron ne jeet hasil kii he
 In the general elections that followed (1967, 1971, 1977, 1980), the Congress won 4 consecutive times
 is bich anti rama raav ne congress se alag hokar ek nai party telugu desham party kii sthapana kii or 1984 ke aam chunaav main congress ke ummidavaar ko haraaya
 After this, there was a tussle between Congress and TDP
 1989 main hue aam chunaavon main congress ne vaapasi kii or phir 1998 tak hue chaar chunaavon lagaataar chaar baar jeet hasil kii
 After this, in 1999, TDP once again wrested this seat from Congress
 lekin wo apane jeet ko ek silsilen tabadil karne main naakaam rahi or 2004 va 2009 main congress ne lagaataar do baar is seat par kabja karne main safalataa hasil kii
 However, in 2014 the YSR Congress candidate won
 saamaajik taana-banise seat par kareeb 15 lakh matadaata hai, jinamein purushon kii sankhya 7,36,216 he or mahila matadaataaon kii sankhya 7,33,891 he
 82 in this seat in the 2014 general election
 23 fisadi logon ne vot daalaa
 This seat was the highest voting percentage in the history so far
 saat vidhansabha vaale is loksabhaa main tidipi kaa palada baari najar aata he
 It has TDP in four assemblies (darsi, Ongole, Kondapi and Kanigiri) and YSR Congress mlas in three assemblies (yerragondapalem, Markapuram and Giddalur)
 is loksabhaa main do vidhansabha (yaragondalim or kondpi) anusuchit jati ke liye arakshit hai
 2014 mandate In the 2014 general election, Ongole Lok Sabha seat was won by sitting MP YV Subba Reddy and defeated tdp's Ummdivar Srinivasulu Reddy by a close margin of 15,658 votes

 Political Background: Jajpur Lok Sabha seat is reserved for Scheduled Castes
 is seat se abtak bijedy, congress or janata dal ke candidet chune gaye hai
 Congress's Ram Chandra Mallik won this seat in the 1962 Lok Sabha elections
 1967 main yahaan se piespi ke bi behera chunaav jite
 This seat came to the Congress account in 1971
 1977 main ram chandra mallik bldi ke tikat par chunaav jite
 Anandi Charan Das won the Lok Sabha elections of 1980, 84, 89, 91 four times in a row
 1996 main janata dal ke anchal das ko jeet mili
 In 1998, Congress candidate Ram Chandra Mallik won the election
 1999 main is seat par bijedy ne entry kii or party candidet jagannatha malik ne chunaav jeeta

 2014 main party candidet reeta tarai ne sava teen lakh voton se jeet hasil kii
 Mythological significance of Jajpur The Jajpur region of Odisha is a place of historical and mythological importance

 This place is nowadays known as 'jajpur'

 is baat khulaasa police ne jaanch ke baad kiya he

 gudgaanv se tees kilometre dur pataudi ilaake ke mandipura gaanv main bandook nok par do mahilaon ke saath chaar din pehle lutpaat aurasamuhik balaatkaaraki vaardaat ko anjaam diya gaya tha
 The accused in the incident is still out of the reach of the police
 jabaki police ne khulaasa kiya he ki badmaashon kaa shikaar bani donon mahilaayein garbhvatee hai
 Both victims are troubled by insecurity and insult
 jaankaree ke mutabik donon peeditaayen apane ghar lautnaa chaahati hai
 But they are afraid that after getting exposed from the case, the accused should not kill their husband and the unborn child
 vaardaat ke baad disipi krime sumit kahaad ke netritv bani esaiti aropiyon ke giraftaari ke gudgaanv samet aas-paas ke jilon main chhapemari kar rahi he
 Apart from this, inputs are also being collected from Uttar Pradesh
 hairaani kii baat ye he ki police ke haath abhi tak koi suraag nahin laga he
 Significantly, on Saturday night at around 12
30 pm, seven to eight number of miscreants attacked a factory in a secluded area
 vahaan bandook kii nok par badmaashon ne company ke workaron se lutpaat kii thi or domahilaonse samuhik balaatkaar bhi kiya tha

 is maamle main haryana mahila ayog kii team bhi maukey kaa daura karne vaali he
 In the world, the seekers must have given each other unbeknownst and how many unique gifts
 lekin aaj baat duniya ke sabase ajeeb tohfe kii
 On the wedding anniversary, a husband gave such a gift to the wife, so that the wife stood directly on the threshold of death
 maut bhi ek jatke main nahin, balki til-til kar or kishton main
 This was a very special day in the life of Arvind and Sonia as both were married a year ago on this day
 sonia ke paas khush hone kii dohari vajah thi
 The first reason was due to marriage anniversary and secondly to the happiness of Arvind, a husband who has been uprooted continuously since his marriage
 kyonki saalagirah ke maukey par arvind thodaa zyada hi khush or badla-badla sa lag rahaa tha
 When the two were married a year ago on 15 February 2012, everything was fine
 lekin dhire-dhire na jane kyon sonia main arvind kaa interest lagaataar kam hota gaya or phir ek vakt aisa bhi aayaa ki jab wo sonia se baat karne se bhi bachane laga
 Sonia feels that perhaps on the occasion of the anniversary, her husband has forgotten all the grievances of his heart, but he was just pretending to be happy
 uske dimag main sajeesh kaa ek aisa khaufnak keedaa kulbula rahaa tha, jiske baahar aate hi donon kii jindagi main bhuuchaal much saktaa tha or badakismati se hua bhi thik vaisaa hi
 
 
 
 or wo tohfasaalagirah kii tamaam baton ke bich arvind ne sonia ko ek ajeeb tohfe kii peshkash kii
 Arvind tells Sonia that since her father has a disease of blood sugar, he does not want her to ever have diabetes, so he wants to give Sonia not just an injection to avoid the disease and a little blood to check
 Also wants to take a sample
 arvind khud hi ek medical lab technitian tha isliye sonia ke paas hairaan hone yaa phir isse manaa karne kii koi vajah nahin thi
 Sonia agreed to take the injection and Arvind dissolved her wife's veins through the same injection
 darasal, ye injection kisi dawa kaa nahin, balki duniya kii sabase ghaatak bimariyon main se ek yani echivi infected ek aisi sui kaa tha ki jiske khun main milane kaa sidhaa sa matlab tha- maut
 The vicious Arvind had now injected her with death to get rid of his wife
 lekin use apni bivi kii maut kii kuch itani jaldi thi ki wo bagaiyr vakt gavaayen is injection kaa asar dekhnaa chahta tha
 Now he plotted another plot for this
 kya thi pati-patni main duriyon kii vajahek central security agency main lab technician ke taur par kaam karne vaale arvind or sonia kii shaadi dhoomdhaam se hui thi
 Sonia's family members did not have any shortcoming in their marriage, but for Sonia, this happiness of marriage could not last for long
 kuch maheene baad hi arvind dhire-dhire apni bivi sonia se duuri banane laga
 In fact, Arvind started coming closer to another girl at his workplace away from Sonia's eyes
 donon ghanton naa sirf milane or baaten karne lage the, balki ek nai jindagi ke khwab bhi bunane lage the
 Arvind now wanted to get rid of Sonia
 magar, musiibat ye thi ki sonia jaisi acchhee patni se talaak lene kii uske paas koi vajah nahin thi
 Being a lab technician, he knew how to extract blood and inject
 ittefaq se kai baar lab main echivi infections kaa maamla bhi aata tha
 Just here, one day something came to his mind that he devised the most terrifying way to get rid of Sonia
 usne apane lab se pehle ek echivi infected sui hasil kii or thik apni shaadi ke ek saal baad yani saalagirah ke roj dhokhe se usne ye sui sonia ko laga diya
 Sonia now gradually became ill due to another deep chalsui
 jabaki arvind usase lagaataar dooriyaan banaata rahaa
 Then one day he plotted another plot
 is baar usne sonia ko bahalane ke baad use ek doosraa injection lagane kaa jhansa diya
